German-Austrian-Swiss Returned Students Association Hosts Farewell Tea for Ambassador Cheng at the International Hotel Yesterday 85

Our country's first ambassador to Germany, Cheng Tianfang, upon receiving his orders, is scheduled to depart for his post within days. The Shanghai German-Austrian-Swiss Returned Students Association and the Tongji University Alumni Association, in particular, held a tea party at the International Hotel on Park Road yesterday afternoon at four o'clock to bid him farewell. Those in attendance included Ambassador Cheng and the embassy secretary Chen Zehua, German Consul General Bai Rende, German Chamber of Commerce President Bo Ersun, General Manager Fu Kaier, German Engineers Association President Tie Meng, German Overseas Chinese Association President Wei De, Manfulanfu China College Friendship Association Quan Congde, Far East Society Grande, and over fifty others. Chairman Weng Zilong gave a farewell speech, followed by a reply from Ambassador Cheng. Both speeches were translated into German by Shen Yi. The text of the two speeches is recorded below:

Chairman's Speech

During the session, Chairman Weng Zilong delivered a farewell speech, which briefly stated: "Today, the German-Austrian-Swiss Returned Students Association and the Tongji University Alumni Association in Shanghai are holding a grand farewell reception to bid farewell to Mr. Cheng Tianfang, our country's first ambassador to Germany. We are honored to have Mr. Cheng grace us with his presence, and also to have Chinese and German guests participate. Mr. Cheng is someone we have always admired. He is a leader of China's cultural movement and a leader in academic and educational circles. It is a great pleasure for us to be able to witness Mr. Cheng's brilliance at this farewell gathering. During the May Fourth Movement, Mr. Cheng led the movement in Shanghai and later studied in the United States and worked for the overseas party headquarters. After returning to China, he held important positions in the central government. In recent years, he has served in political positions in Jiangsu and Anhui provinces and presided over National Zhejiang University and the Central Political School, making many contributions to the country and society. Now that Mr. Cheng is appointed as our country's first ambassador to Germany, he will certainly be fully competent, which is beyond doubt. The cultures of various countries are different, but each has its own unique points. In recent years, Germans have conducted a lot of research on Chinese academic studies, and the number of Chinese people going to Germany to study science is also increasing daily. From this perspective, the communication of Chinese and German cultures is very important. With Mr. Cheng's past contributions to culture, the communication of Chinese and German cultures will certainly have greater development in the future, which is beyond doubt. We know that the special spirit of our Chinese nation is 'loving peace and emphasizing trustworthiness,' and the special spirit of the German nation is 'burying oneself in hard work and striving for construction.' We hope that Mr. Cheng can bring our spirit of emphasizing trustworthiness and loving peace to Germany and spread it throughout Europe to maintain lasting international peace. At the same time, we hope that he can bring back the German spirit of burying oneself in hard work and striving for construction as a good example for our construction of a new China."

Ambassador Cheng's Reply

After Chairman Weng Zilong finished his speech, Ambassador Cheng stood up and replied, briefly stating: "I am honored and ashamed to be invited to this gathering hosted by the Shanghai German-Austrian-Swiss Returned Students Association and the Tongji University Alumni Association. This time, the central government has appointed me as the ambassador to Germany. I am deeply aware that my talent and ability are insufficient and that I have failed to live up to the trust of the central government. The Chinese people, influenced by the thoughts of the ancient sages, have always regarded peace as the main purpose in dealing with foreign countries. China's current foreign policy, I dare to say, is to maintain friendship with all friendly countries in the world. However, the relationship between China and Germany is particularly different, precisely because the two countries have recently shared a similar history. The oppression and economic panic suffered by the Germans after the European War were no less than our current situation. In my opinion, the difficulties Germany faced at that time may have been even greater than China's current situation. Therefore, many people were worried about Germany and did not know what the outcome would be. However, because of the hard work and struggle of the German government and people, they were able to turn danger into safety and emerge from a difficult environment onto a bright path. All undertakings are thriving and admired by people all over the world. China has also recently encountered an extremely difficult environment, and the Chinese government and people are also working hard and striving to implement national recovery measures. Therefore, we see the achievements of Germany's struggle and increase our infinite courage. German friends, seeing the facts of our efforts, will certainly express infinite sympathy. Because of this reason, although China and Germany are of different races and cultures, their relationship is naturally particularly close. After the mutual dispatch of ambassadors this time, the relationship between the two countries will definitely become closer. I am also willing to do my best to promote this aspect. I will be leaving the country soon, and I hope you will continue to give me guidance in the future. I wish you all good health and the Sino-German cultural cause a bright future."

Cai Took the Haiheng Steamer to Qingdao Yesterday Morning

After learning that President Wang had submitted his resignation, the Central Government entrusted a friend who came to Shanghai from Beijing to convey the instruction to persuade Wang to stay. Industrial and Commercial Loan Association Suggests Flexible Guarantee Methods; Credit Loan Shop Guarantees Changed to One; Two Cases Each Borrowing 200 Yuan Have Been Approved 87

The Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee held its seventh meeting recently and approved two small credit loan cases. The remaining 18 cases were rejected or notified to change the guarantee due to non-compliance with the procedures. Eleven cases are still under investigation. The association, considering that it is practically difficult for various factories and shops to find two shop guarantees, decided to suggest to the Ministry of Finance to change it to one. The details are recorded separately below:

Committee Approved Two Loan Cases

At 4:00 p.m. the day before yesterday (the 9th), the seventh meeting was held at the National Goods Bank. The committee members present were Cai Zengji, Qin Runqing, Song Ziliang, Wang Yansong, Wang Xiaolai, Bei Songsun, Chen Guangfu, Zhang Peishen (replaced by Bei Songsun), Xi Demao, and Du Yuesheng (replaced by Wang Xiaolai), totaling ten people. In addition to the chairman Cai Zengji reporting on the daily affairs of the association, four loan applications that had been investigated and reviewed were submitted for discussion. It was decided that Guangming Battery Industrial Cooperative and Yongtai Candy Store would each be approved to borrow 200 yuan. Zhou Fuji Embroidery Store's request to borrow 5,000 yuan was approved to be reviewed again after changing to a proper guarantee. Senji Paper Mill's request to borrow 5,000 yuan was rejected because the guarantor was found to be ineligible. It is reported that the association had received a total of 21 applications for a total of 53,930 yuan as of the 9th. Among them, 16 cases were rejected because they did not comply with the principles of lending and the detailed rules of lending (such as not operating national goods and falsely filling out forms, and not having actual equity guarantees). The remaining 15 cases were investigated. After investigation, the above-mentioned four cases were decided by the meeting. The rest will be decided at the next meeting.

Suggest to the Ministry of Finance to Reduce Shop Guarantees

The Loan Committee, based on the ten principles of lending stipulated by the ministry, stipulates that credit loans must be guaranteed by two substantial commercial firms. Based on recent facts, the committee felt that it was difficult for the factories and shops applying for loans to find two shop guarantees in this economic downturn. In order to take care of industry and commerce and provide effective relief, it was reported that it had been decided to suggest to the Ministry of Finance to change the two shop guarantees specified in the ten principles to one shop guarantee. It must wait until the ministry's order is approved and implemented.

Noodle Company Industry Changes Procedures

In addition, the Noodle Company Association recently sent a letter to the Noodle Market Industry Association, requesting loans of 100 yuan, 50 yuan, and 30 yuan to the member stores of the association, and changing the guarantee procedures, proposing to use three-party joint guarantees certified by the association. The Loan Association was asked to review it. It was also decided at the meeting to allow the change, and the loan will be approved after consulting with the Ministry of Finance. The original letter reads: "Respectfully, according to a letter from the Noodle Company Industry Association on the 6th of this month, it was found that there are no less than hundreds of stores in the city run by members of the association, with capital ranging from several hundred yuan to over a thousand yuan. Before January 28th, there were over 500 stores. After the war, due to the economic downturn, most of them suffered losses and could not maintain their operations, and have closed down. Now there are only over 200 stores left. If we continue to sit idly by, they will all close down. Fortunately, your association has industrial and commercial credit small loans, which can truly give all members of the association hope for Chong Qing Lai Su. However, most member stores are small businesses, and can be divided into three grades. Grade A has capital of 1,000 yuan, Grade B has capital of 500 yuan, and Grade C has capital of over 300 yuan. It is proposed that Grade A borrow 100 yuan, Grade B borrow 50 yuan, and Grade C borrow 30 yuan. According to the methods promulgated by your association, there must be two substantial commercial firms as guarantors, but the members of the association are small businesses, so it is proposed to use three-party joint guarantees and be certified by the association to show credit, and to separately formulate a repayment plan. Is this feasible? We still ask for your approval so that we can start to implement it. It is a great convenience, etc." Upon receipt, it was found that it was not easy to find guarantees from two actual equity commercial firms for the small business of the industry. In order to implement the purpose of rescuing small industry and commerce, this provision should be changed accordingly. We hereby send a letter to your association to request your review and reply so that we can forward it. This is the most important thing. Respectfully to the Shanghai Industrial and Commercial Loan Review Committee."

Commissioner Liang's Talk on His Return from Inspecting South Africa: Studying the Causes of the Mistreatment of Overseas Chinese; Detailed Listing of the Shortcomings of Chinese Merchants That Should Be Remedied 91

Guomin News Agency reported that Liang Yugao, a commissioner sent by the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to South Africa to inspect consulates and overseas Chinese affairs and to investigate commercial affairs, along with his secretary Xu Kuibo, departed from Shanghai on April 11th. After four months of inspection, they have completed their mission and returned home on the Dutch liner Swartenhondt. The ship docked at Wusongkou the night before last, and arrived in Shanghai at 8:00 a.m. this morning. Friends and relatives of the two had received telegrams in advance and went to welcome them, which was very lively. The reporter, upon hearing the news, also drove to visit them. According to Liang's statement, as follows:

This Trip Lasted Four Months

He went to many places, including the Near East, Africa, the British island of Mauritius, where there are about 8,000 overseas Chinese; the French island of Reunion, where there are about 2,000 overseas Chinese; the French island of Madagascar, where there are about 3,000 overseas Chinese; the British island of Mayotte near Comoros, where there are about 200 overseas Chinese; the Portuguese East African cities of Lourenço Marques and Beira, where there are about 400 overseas Chinese each; the Union of South Africa, where there are about 3,000 overseas Chinese; and other small islands in the Indian Ocean, some with hundreds of overseas Chinese, some with dozens of overseas Chinese, and some with less than ten overseas Chinese, such as the British island of Sansibar and the British East African city of Mombasa. It is true that the footprints of overseas Chinese are all over the world. The overseas Chinese in the above-mentioned places deeply regret that they are far away from their motherland and that news is extremely isolated. However, they can all understand the international status and foreign policy of their motherland, and their patriotism is the same as that of overseas Chinese all over the world. It is a pity that their culture is low and they lack talent.

Efforts Should Be Made to Remedy It

The overseas Chinese in the above-mentioned places are all from Guangdong and are mostly engaged in the grocery business, followed by carpentry and planting. Their economic situation is relatively good compared to overseas Chinese in the Union of South Africa. The others are not as good. The Union of South Africa is a gold-producing country, so it cannot avoid the impact of the economic downturn, but it is better than most countries in the world. However, the Union government imposes various unequal treatments on Asians and people of color in terms of law and society, which is unparalleled in any country in the world, such as immigration, rental, business, drinking, and transportation and entertainment. All the rights enjoyed by whites are absolutely not enjoyed by Asians and people of color (with some exceptions). Unfortunately, our Republic of China is located in Asia, and the Chinese nation is yellow, which has resulted in our overseas Chinese being subjected to double oppression, especially the more than 2,000 overseas Chinese living in Johannesburg (the gold-producing area) in the Transvaal province of the Union of South Africa and Pretoria, the capital of the Union of South Africa. We will report to the government in detail and find ways to negotiate the cancellation of it. We are studying

The Reasons Why the Union Mistreats Our Overseas Chinese

And the complex situation of the overseas Chinese in the Union, so we need to conduct various investigations, and guide the improvement of the consulate's affairs and the investigation of commercial affairs, so we spent more time in Johannesburg and Pretoria in the Union of South Africa, and the round trip also took 70 days. Therefore, we did not have time to go to Mumbai, Calcutta, and Yangon for inspection as originally planned. We received an urgent telegram from the government urging us to return to prepare for the Sino-Burmese border demarcation. As for international trade, there is great potential for development in the Union of South Africa, such as tea (Shanghai Wang Yutai's Qimen black tea sells very well), lace, silk embroidery, Lanzhou (Shandong Shangzhuang also has a good business), silk fabrics, clothing, porcelain, carpets, etc. can be promoted. Most of the Union of South Africa's imports are from Germany, but most of the import and export merchants are Jews, and the Jews strongly resist German goods, so although the Union government has a trade agreement with Germany, it cannot sell its goods. The Jews believe that the Japanese dumping policy is unfair, so they do not promote it. Moreover, the Union of South Africa does not welcome Japanese goods very much. It is common to see signs in front of stores that say "No Japanese goods sold here." Therefore, Chinese goods can be promoted in Africa. As for the wine and brandy in the Union of South Africa, although they are not as good as those produced in France, the price is very reasonable. The tobacco leaves are of good quality and the price is very cheap. We can also try to sell other products such as wool, raisins, fresh fruits, and salted fish. The politicians of the Union of South Africa have recently adopted a policy of gradually breaking away from the shackles of British rule and are eager to find new markets in the world. If our country can mutually sell goods with them, so that friendly relations can be enhanced, it is also a way to eliminate the mistreatment of our overseas Chinese. I have paid special attention to

Commercial Affairs on This Trip

Indeed, the number of our people overseas is increasing every year, and there is no way to reduce it. We have to seek the development of overseas trade in order to make up for it. Therefore, wherever I went, I talked to the general import and export merchants. They are all very willing to promote our country's goods, but they are very dissatisfied with our manufacturers. I will list them as follows, and I hope that if there is anything to be changed, change it, and if there is nothing to be commended, commend it. (1) They cannot pay attention to the credibility of the goods. Our country's goods are not without a market, but our manufacturers lack credibility. The goods sent are often not consistent with the samples, and when they write to inquire, there is no reply. In this case, there is only one transaction, and they dare not ask about it again. (2) The miscalculation of raising the price of goods. Some manufacturers, when they encounter overseas orders, think it is a good opportunity to make a fortune, and arbitrarily raise the price of goods. They do not know that the orderers are experienced and have a good understanding of the quality of goods and the level of prices. Therefore, there is no possibility of continued transactions. (3) The fallacy of gradually increasing the price of goods. When ordering goods from our country's manufacturers, the price of the same goods is different from the first batch, and the price of the second and third batches is different, often increasing batch by batch, which makes it very difficult for sellers. If they increase the price accordingly, they will be questioned by the buyers. If they do not increase the price, they will have no reason to sell at a loss, so they stop trading and no longer act as agents for promotion. (4) The samples are not exquisite and must be paid for. The reason why Japanese goods can sell well is entirely due to the power of giving away exquisite samples. Taking cloth as an example, one side shows the white cloth body, and the other side lists various colors, and the original price and shipping cost are clearly marked in detail. The English term is (C.J.F.jnStirling). The samples of Chinese goods are not only not as exquisite as Japanese goods, but some manufacturers do not allow them to be given away and must be paid for, which is a deterrent to those who argue for goods. (5) The packaging is too sloppy. Our country's manufacturers do not seem to pay much attention to the packaging of goods. Most of them think that the packaging is finished, and do not consider how to pack it so that it will not be lost, damaged, or damp. The orderers often suffer this loss, and the negotiation is ineffective, resulting in the cessation of transactions. (6) Prices should be converted into British currency (Stirling Quotation). Commerce in Africa is based on British shillings, and there are no exchange rate tables available for checking the conversion of Shanghai, Hong Kong, and other currencies. When orderers write to inquire about the price of goods, our manufacturers do not know the reason and often reply with the price in national currency or Hong Kong currency, which makes it impossible to calculate. Even if they want to engage in purchasing, they have no way to start. In general, our manufacturers can easily improve the above-mentioned shortcomings, and my greatest impression on this trip is that Japanese goods are everywhere, and wherever there is traffic and densely populated places, such as train stations, there are Japanese goods on display, so that people unconsciously caress and visit. In Beira, East Africa, I heard that only one Japanese ship used to arrive every month, but now there are four or five ships, and Japanese goods are piled up like mountains, and the natives compete to buy them. I deeply sigh at their business methods, which are like mercury pouring on the ground, and there is no hole that they do not enter. We should imitate them. Our country's manufacturers suffer from the lack of large capital, so there are many shortcomings in the promotion methods, and it is difficult to compete with others. The plan for today is to hope that people who are enthusiastic about engaging in commercial affairs will gather strong capital and organize a

Large-Scale Company

Link up with various factories and act as the general agent for each factory, and work hard to develop overseas trade. Externally, (1) organize overseas national goods mobile exhibitions to promote them, (2) send overseas salesmen to widely solicit customers, as close as the Philippines, the British Malay Peninsula, and the Dutch East Indies, and as far as Africa and the islands in the Indian Ocean, round and round. Once commercial affairs are promoted, the international status can also be increased. Internally, study the conformity of goods and samples, the balance of prices, the improvement of samples and (C.L.F in Slirling) the detailed price list, the proper packaging, and the conversion of our country's currency system and the currency systems of various countries in the price, so that it is easy to calculate, and the company is absolutely responsible to the orderers. Other advertising promotions are also planned by the company, but all factories must obey the company's orders, and the company's profits are to extract certain commissions from the sales of certain factory's goods. With this method, it is expected that the results will be considerable. The key to doing business is to take the initiative to find people, not to wait for people to come to find us, and especially to win people's hearts, so that we can benefit step by step. It is heard that Mr. Liang will rest in Shanghai for one day before returning to Beijing to report on his mission.

New Initiatives in Shipping 92

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company Hosted Press Yesterday

The state-owned China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, under orders to implement a new lifestyle movement on its ships, dispatched committee members from the Nanchang New Life Movement General Association to Shanghai for instructions. It was decided to start with training the stewards to gradually promote the movement and eradicate existing bad habits on the ships. Yesterday, Liu Hongsheng, General Manager of the company, and Committee Member Yan, hosted a banquet for the press at the YMCA on Ba Xian Qiao Road. Over forty reporters from various newspapers attended. The two gentlemen reported on the progress of the initiative. The following is a summary:

Mr. Liu's Report

Mr. Liu's report stated, in brief, that since the New Life Movement was initiated by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek, it has been promoted in various regions. Last year, the General Association sent personnel to Shanghai to inspect the orderliness and cleanliness of the company's ships and docks. Many suggestions for reform were offered, and the current state of the stewards on the ships was deemed in urgent need of reform. The Ministry of Communications has repeatedly issued instructions for the company to rectify the stewards, but due to deeply ingrained habits, no results have been achieved. This April, the Ministry of Communications approved a telegram from the Military Affairs Commission Chairman’s Headquarters, forwarding the regulations for implementing the new shipping lifestyle movement to the company for implementation. In July, the General Association decided to first establish a New Life Training Class for stewards within the company, using the training of stewards as a starting point for promoting the new movement on all ships. Simultaneously, the General Association sent personnel to the company to discuss implementation. Currently, the preparations for the training class are largely complete. For the first class, one hundred and twenty stewards from the Xin Jiangtian ship will be selected to come ashore for training. Subsequently, other ships will be included in turn. The training period is two months. After the training, the company will assign them to positions accordingly. After receiving training, the stewards' service will undoubtedly be superior to before, directly satisfying passengers and indirectly providing a more secure guarantee for the stewards' livelihoods.

Mr. Yan's Speech

Following Mr. Liu, Mr. Yan delivered a speech, stating that since the New Life Movement was promoted by Chairman Chiang Kai-shek in February of last year, it has been implemented in nineteen provincial capitals, the three major commercial ports of Beijing, Shanghai, and Tianjin, over eight hundred counties nationwide, and on various state-owned railways. However, shipping has been lacking. Chinese shipping has deeply ingrained bad habits, and if not improved, the future will be unimaginable. The General Association, recognizing this, first conducted an investigation and gathered opinions from various shipping companies. A plan for implementation was formulated, and he was dispatched to Shanghai to coordinate the effort. It has now been decided to start with steward training, and preparations are complete with the first training class about to begin. However, as this is a new initiative, there are bound to be misunderstandings from the outside, and the stewards on various ships may believe that there will be large-scale layoffs. However, the company is truly trying to improve the lives and income of each individual and provide them with valuable service skills. During his visit to Shanghai, he received assistance from all parties, which allowed the project to proceed smoothly, and he is deeply optimistic about the future of the New Life Movement. It is said that Mr. Yan will return to Jiangxi via Beijing within a few days to report on the progress.

Package Joint Transportation by Two Railways and Three Motor Vehicle Companies 93

Contract Amendment Agreed Upon - Effective September 1st

The joint passenger transportation service between the two railways and the Xiao Shao, Shao Cao Sheng, and Hao Xin three motor vehicle companies in Sheng County and Xinchang had previously been contracted and implemented since January 1, 1935. Now, the said company has requested to add package joint transportation. The railway bureau, to facilitate merchants' shipment of goods, has negotiated an amendment to the contract. The New News Agency reporter has recorded the provisions as follows: Jinghu, Huhangyong Railway Administration, Xiao Shao Motor Vehicle Co., Ltd., Shao Cao Sheng Motor Vehicle Road Co., Ltd., Hao Xin Road Motor Vehicle Co., Ltd. Passenger Joint Transportation Contract Attachment. (1) To facilitate merchants' shipment of goods, joint package transportation will be added starting September 1, 1935. This attachment is added to the original contract and must be followed by all four parties. (2) The validity period of this attachment shall be the same as the validity period of the original contract. (3) The railway bureau's charging method for transporting packages is as follows: within 50 kilometers, 7 li per kilogram; within 100 kilometers, 1.4 fen per kilogram; within 150 kilometers, 2.1 fen per kilogram; within 200 kilometers, 2.8 fen per kilogram. The maximum weight per package is 60 kilograms, and the maximum volume is 185 cubic decimeters. The minimum charge per package is 2 jiao. (4) The charging method for company packages: Xiao Shao, Shao Cao Sheng, and Hao Xin three companies shall all charge 4 li per kilogram per 10 kilometers. Any distance less than 10 kilometers shall be calculated as 10 kilometers. The mileage of each party shall be calculated separately and not combined. The maximum weight per package is 60 kilograms, and the maximum volume is 185 cubic decimeters. If the weight or volume exceeds these limits and cannot be transported by motor vehicle, both parties shall refuse to load the package. The minimum freight rate for each package shall be 2 jiao for each party. (5) Fees for crossing the river, porterage, etc., shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 11 of the contract. (6) The procedures for receiving and delivering packages at Nanxingqiao Station shall be handled in accordance with the provisions of Article 10 of the contract. (7) If a package is lost within the railway bureau's jurisdiction, the railway bureau shall compensate according to railway regulations. If a package is lost within the company's jurisdiction, the company shall compensate according to railway regulations. If it cannot be determined which party is responsible for the loss, the amount of compensation shall be apportioned by each party in proportion to the revenue received from the joint transportation of that item. (8) Any matters not specified in this attachment shall be governed by the various provisions of the original contract.

Tragic Drowning of Four Lives Under the New Rubbish Bridge in Suzhou Creek 94

Caused by Lounging on the Same Plank, Which Broke and Led to Drowning

A tragic drowning occurred yesterday afternoon at 1:40 under the New Rubbish Bridge in Suzhou Creek, claiming four lives. The Datong News Agency reporter has made a special effort to record the situation as follows:

Lounging on a Plank

There are many civilian boats docked along Suzhou Creek. These boats, commonly known as "Wudu boats," are inhabited by laborers who go ashore to work during the day and return to their boats to sleep at night. Their parents and families live on the boats, no different from a floating family. Yesterday afternoon at 1:40, under the north side of the New Rubbish Bridge in Suzhou Creek, which is where these boats congregate, planks were used to connect the boats for passage. At that time, the housewife of a Chen family boat (31 years old, from Yancheng) was relaxing on a plank with her 20-year-old eldest daughter and 4-year-old youngest daughter. Soon after, another housewife from a Zhang family boat (43 years old, same origin) also brought her 10+-year-old daughter to relax on the same plank.

Plank Breaks

Not long after, a boy named Wu Xiaogui (11 years old) from a boat (docked in front of the Bank of China warehouse) from Taizhou also walked onto the plank to relax. The plank, which was very thin and fragile, could not bear the weight of six people and suddenly broke, causing all six to fall into the water. The river in that area had recently been deepened by dredging ships sent by the Dredging Bureau, so after the six fell into the water, only the Zhang family boat housewife and the Chen family boat housewife's eldest daughter immediately resurfaced and were rescued. The other four sank deep into the water. Despite the best efforts of neighboring boats to rescue them, nothing was found until after 4 PM, when the crew members of the various boats finally retrieved them from under the boats. However, all four had already drowned.

Two Rescued

After the bodies were recovered, they were immediately transported by boat to the Neilu Jiaozui Water Patrol Station for reporting to the authorities for inspection. At the same time, the family members of the various boats were also summoned for questioning. When the Datong News Agency reporter went to the boats to investigate at around 7 PM last night, they had not yet been released.

Using a Hired Woman as a Puppet to Cheat Five Dou of Rice 96

Zengtai Rice Shop Defrauded - Lin Changshi Granted Bail

Recently, the hearts of people in Shanghai have become increasingly treacherous, and the tricks of fraud have become even more bizarre. In front of the Zengtai Rice Shop at No. 130 Bailinan Road in Western Shanghai, a man wearing a silk shirt, about thirty years old, suddenly arrived with a simple-looking middle-aged female servant on the afternoon before yesterday. He claimed to be buying five dou of high-quality white rice, worth six yuan, and asked the old store clerk to deliver the rice and bring back the money. The shop then ordered Zhang Xingfu, an employee, to follow with the rice. When they reached near Zhaofeng Garden, the man suddenly said to Zhang, "This rice is being bought on behalf of a cohabitant, so I need to open a receipt. You put the rice down by the roadside temporarily, and I'll watch it here. Luckily, it's not far. You go quickly and open it. If you're worried, you can order the servant to go with you." Zhang believed that with the servant accompanying him, he could trust him, so he immediately took the woman back to the shop to get the receipt. However, when he returned, the man was nowhere to be seen. Zhang then twisted the woman back to the shop to report what happened. When questioned, the woman claimed that her name was Lin Changshi, 35 years old, from Wujiang. She had just arrived in Shanghai from her hometown. At noon today, the man, who claimed to be the master of the house, hired a female servant from the Hang hiring agency opposite the Gengxin Theater in Zhabei. He told me to follow him to his residence to help as a servant. He took a taxi, and I took a rickshaw. We went to Great British Road, then changed to a tram and came here to call for rice. I really don't know where the master went. His address is written on a note left at the hiring agency. The shop, believing that she was in cahoots to swindle the rice, immediately called the police to detain her at the Caojiadu Branch. After the officers questioned her separately, they ordered Detective Tu Yixin to go to the hiring agency to inquire. According to the agency, the man behaved generously and, after coming to select Lin Changshi, said that since her home was far away at No. 41 Donghan Bili Road in Hongkou, he wrote a note with the address and left it there, instructing her to follow him. The officer then went to Donghan Bili Road according to the address and found that the address was a pawnshop, indicating that the man's fraudulent scheme was extremely clever. He returned to the bureau to report. Since there was insufficient evidence to prove that the defendant woman was in cahoots, she was granted bail separately. It is hoped that all shops in Shanghai will pay attention and be cautious.

Telephone Company's Bills - Cannot Charge Those Who Did Not Make Calls 101

-Taxpayer Society Sends Letters to Four Groups-

The Shanghai Concession Chinese Taxpayer Society sent letters yesterday to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, the First Special District Citizens' Federation, the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, and the French Concession Chinese Taxpayer Society, stating: We are writing to inform you that the Shanghai Telephone Company's bills often include a charge of five jiao or several jiao for users connected to the Shanghai Telephone Bureau. Our association has often received protests regarding this matter. Therefore, on July 12th, we sent a letter to the Public Concession Public Works Department, instructing the company to record the following facts on the toll bills and not to be ambiguous or use trickery: (1) Date, (2) Time, (3) Telephone number called, (4) Connected or not connected, (5) Call duration. Such records would allow users to understand where their number is, and it would be easy to investigate whether they have any contact or familiarity with users of those numbers. For those who never used that type of call and have declared so in writing, the company should immediately remove the charge and, in the future, not connect their phone to users of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau who request such connections. In this way, users can avoid suffering illegal losses and make the company respect users' intentions and avoid the suspicion of illegal income. If the company's bills do not list these items clearly, then according to commercial practice, there should be a legal right to verify them. If the company continues to include these toll charges on the bill after the user has declared that they do not need this type of call, then it should be considered a separate act and cannot be recovered from innocent parties. Users should not suffer in silence because the amount is small and the negotiation is troublesome. Even small legal interests should not be lost. As this matter concerns the public interest, we are writing to your associations, requesting that you inform your members so that they may protect their legal rights and promote public welfare.

Youth Jumps into the Sea from the Xin Ningshao Ship, Leaving Behind a 19-Year-Old Widow - Smiled at Her Before Dying - Family Devastated by the News - No Need for Suicide, Truly a Sin 104

Romantic Nature

City Chamber of Commerce Letter to the Bureau of Finance: Requesting Flexible Methods for Self-Payment of House Tax 105

Shanghai and Wusong Are Forty to Fifty Li Apart; Time and Economic Losses Are Significant

The Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce sent a letter to the Municipal Bureau of Finance yesterday, stating: "Respectfully, on the 9th of this month, according to a letter from our Wusong branch, it stated that our branch recently received a joint letter from various businesses, stating: 'Respectfully, we find that although the Wusong area is under the jurisdiction of Shanghai, it is quite far from the prosperous area of Shanghai. Therefore, various administrative agencies of the city have personnel stationed in Wusong to facilitate matters and care for the common people. The merchants and residents of Wusong praise this convenience. The same applies to the Bureau of Finance's collection of house tax. Collectors are stationed in Wusong year-round to collect taxes. However, this month, a notice from the Shanghai Municipal Bureau of Finance suddenly ordered that, starting from the autumn term of the fourteenth year of the Republic, all those with a house tax of ten yuan or more must pay it themselves to the Shanghai Municipal Bank, and it is limited to be paid from the 1st of this month to the 10th of this month, with a 2% surcharge for late payments. After receiving the order, the merchants were shocked, as Shanghai and Wusong are forty to fifty li apart, and a round trip by boat or car takes no less than five or six hours. The time spent is already extremely uneconomical, and adding the travel expenses to the house tax is even less desirable for the merchants and residents. Furthermore, according to the Bureau of Finance, tax households with less than ten yuan are still being collected by collectors stationed in Wusong. This approach benefits neither the public nor the private sector, and only increases the travel expenses of the common people. Also, according to the original intention of the Bureau of Finance, perhaps it is to reduce the responsibility of the collectors and prevent corruption, so large households are ordered to pay directly to the bank. However, the Wusong area now also has a Xinhua Bank office, and money shops such as Long Mao Zhuang, all of which have outstanding credit and strong financial resources, can be entrusted to collect taxes on behalf of the bureau, just like the Farmers Bank of the Interior collects land taxes and sets up branches in rural areas. Therefore, the merchants and residents believe that the Bureau of Finance's self-payment of house tax is only feasible in areas close to the urban area, and is really inconvenient in the Wusong area. Therefore, they jointly request that your Chamber forward this request to the Bureau of Finance, allowing the old method of sending collectors to collect taxes to continue. If there is concern about collectors engaging in corruption, the bureau can entrust banks or money shops in the Wusong area to collect taxes after issuing notices, so that merchants and residents can pay nearby within the time limit. We look forward to your assistance.' Upon receiving this, we found that at a time when all industries are declining, enabling the common people to spend one less cent unexpectedly means maintaining their livelihood for a little longer. The matters stated by the merchants are true, and the method is also feasible. Accordingly, we hereby report the situation to your Chamber, hoping that you will quickly forward it to the Bureau of Finance and make changes to the collection of house tax in the Wusong area. We truly value our public friendship, etc." Upon receiving this, we found that our Chamber has received letters from the noodle industry and the lumber industry one after another, and has forwarded them to your bureau twice, requesting changes, but we have not received approval. However, in your bureau's reply to the lumber industry, No. 5858, on May 31st, it stated that "convenience will be provided to households paying house tax themselves." Our Chamber believes that in order to implement this principle thoroughly, the time and financial resources of the tax households should be taken into consideration. Now, Shanghai and Wusong are forty to fifty li apart, and a round trip by boat or car takes no less than five or six hours. The time spent is already wasted, and in addition to the house tax, the round-trip travel expenses cause even more economic losses. All of this is inconsistent with the Bureau's so-called principle of facilitating tax households. Moreover, with collectors stationed in Wusong and the self-payment method for tax households coexisting, the government is inevitably wasting salaries, and the collectors are almost like parasites accompanying meals. The so-called "no benefit to both the public and private sectors" by the branch office is indeed a valid argument. If your bureau believes that the Wusong area is relatively far away and the situation is different, canceling the self-payment method for tax households would be greatly appreciated by the merchants and residents of the town. Otherwise, before the Municipal Bank establishes branches in the Wusong area, entrusting other reliable firms to collect taxes nearby would also alleviate the difficulties. Since your bureau's principle for tax households is to facilitate procedures, we urge you to choose one of the two methods requested by our Chamber, reply, and implement it.

Telegram from the Laohekou Public Security Bureau Requesting Relief 106

Duan Wengong, Director of the Public Security Bureau of Laohekou, Hubei, wrote: "To the Editor of the Shanghai Shen Bao: I have learned that Laohekou City was built in the middle of the Qianlong period of the Qing Dynasty. It connects Qin and Long in the north, and Ba and Shu on the sides. It is located upstream of Jing and Xiang, and has long been known as a military town in northern Hubei. In addition, it borders the Han River, with convenient boat transportation, a gathering of products, and a convergence of merchants. The central and local tax revenues, as well as various financial institutions, are also numerous. In the 18th and 19th years of the Republic, the population reached over 100,000, and commerce reached its peak. Recently, it has been affected by the current situation, and the market is depressed, which is very different from the past. Unexpectedly, heaven has not been satisfied with the disaster, and fog and rain have caused calamity. From July 3rd to 7th, it lasted for five days and nights without ceasing. In addition, mountain torrents broke out, and the Han River suddenly poured into the city, turning the entire city into a swamp. The water depth ranged from three or four feet to more than ten feet. Countless houses in the city collapsed, and thousands of thatched houses outside the Huacheng Gate were washed away to the east, leaving only rubble. The flood victims inside and outside the city clung to the roofs and treetops, calling for help, which was unbearable to hear. The Bureau, together with the garrisoned troops, organized rescue teams to rush to rescue them in different ways. It is estimated that more than 9,000 men, women, old, and young have been rescued. They were then selected to be housed in higher places and gathered together. At the same time, gentry and merchants were convened to discuss relief measures, and it was decided to temporarily have the shops and residents with less severe disasters donate congee to barely sustain life. At the same time, letters were sent to various organizations and groups to rush to raise more than 2,000 yuan for emergency relief, which was distributed separately. However, the disaster is extremely serious, and everything is waiting to be rebuilt. It is estimated that more than 200 zhang of the city walls were washed down by the flood, and all the wharves along the coast were swept into the torrent. More than 6,000 houses collapsed, and the number of flood victims who were displaced and cut off from their livelihoods reached more than 10,000, which is truly an unprecedented catastrophe. Now, to implement relief, it is not a work that can be done with a cartload of firewood and a cup of water. Moreover, to plan for the restoration of prosperity, there must be a comprehensive plan. I have long admired the gentlemen of your newspaper for their concern for the people and their compassion, and their enthusiasm for disaster relief in the past. I dare to ask you to have the spirit of treating the hunger of others as your own and the drowning of others as your own, and to fulfill the wish of loving our compatriots and helping them. Call out loudly, and the mountains will respond. The survivors of the disaster can entrust their lives, and the dying business community can be revived. The people will be fortunate, and the region will be fortunate. In addition to requesting the provincial government to quickly provide relief, I am sending thirty-seven photos of the flood with this letter, and I beg you to make plates and publish them daily to show the disaster situation, and I beg you to express your opinions and call for help to all parties. I respectfully lead more than 60,000 citizens to bow nine times to ask, and I respectfully wish you good writing. I hope you will understand. Sincerely, Duan Wengong, Director of the Public Security Bureau of Laohekou, Hubei, July 30th."

Cao Maode Departs for the United States to Discuss Business 108

Departing Today on the Empress of Canada

Mr. Cao Maode, General Manager of the China Mainland Commercial Company, is departing overseas today on the Empress of Canada to discuss business in the United States, Canada, and other places. The company has been operating for seven years and has developed its business. It enjoys a high reputation among the import and export industries run by Chinese people. It was recently designed for the Ministry of Railways to manufacture medicine bridge piers, and it has been publicly tendered to undertake this large batch of wood.

Mr. Cao Maode expects that the railways in Beijing-Shanghai, Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo will use this to expand branch lines. It is believed that China's railways' use of medicinal bridge timber is a pioneer. According to the records of various railways in the United States and Canada, the bridges built with medicinal timber are still in good condition after 50 years of use, and the cost is 40% lower than using iron and concrete. It is said that Mr. Cao's trip will also include an inspection of the forestry industry in Canada, and he is expected to return to China in three months, at which time he will contribute what he has learned to the Chinese people.

In recent years, the China Merchant Electric Tram Company has been making unremitting efforts to develop transportation in Nanshi. Longjiang Road Red Pill Agency Case Judged 110

Hao Yigu, the Chinese Head Constable of the Yulin Road Patrol Room, along with Chinese and Western constables, cracked a red pill agency selling case at 142 Longjiang Road at 9:20 pm the day before yesterday. The chief culprit, Li Abao from Jiangyin, and customers Chen A'gen from Ningbo, Wang Jinbiao from Anhui, suspect Chen Lusheng, and others, a total of 1,000 people, along with smoking utensils and red pills, were taken to the patrol room. Yesterday morning, they were escorted to the Third Criminal Court of the Special First Court. Wang Yaotang, a lawyer from the Bureau of Works, stated the previous situation, and Head Constable Hao reported the details of the case. The exhibits were presented for inspection, and Judge Xiao Xie questioned the defendants. Li Abao was sentenced to one year of imprisonment, Wang Jinbiao was sentenced to 50 days of detention, and Lu A'gen was fined 30 yuan. The exhibits were confiscated according to the list, and Chen Lusheng was acquitted.

Plan for Implementing Compulsory Education (Part Two) 131

— (Speech Broadcast by Lei Zhen on Central Wireless Radio)

5. Teachers

Regarding the issue of teacher training, it is divided into the following categories:

(1) Training of Short-Term Primary School Teachers: After the start of the first phase of compulsory education in each province and city, short-term primary school teacher training classes should be widely established in senior middle schools and normal schools at the provincial, municipal, or county level. Students with a junior middle school education level should be recruited to study primary school teaching materials and teaching methods. After completing the training and passing the examination, they will be given a certificate allowing them to serve as teachers in short-term primary schools.

(2) Training of One-Year Short-Term Primary School Teachers: During the first phase, each province and city should recruit people with fluent writing skills, rich common sense, and a desire to become teachers in short-term primary schools. After passing the examination, they will be given a certificate allowing them to serve as one-year short-term primary school teachers. When necessary, civil servants may be ordered to serve in short-term primary schools.

(3) Training to Improve Private School Teachers: Junior middle schools or normal schools at the county or municipal level, as well as large-scale county primary schools, should establish training classes for private school teachers, recruiting private school teachers to specialize in teaching materials and teaching methods for short-term primary school courses. After short-term training and passing the examination, they will be given a certificate allowing them to serve as improved private school teachers.

(4) Qualification Examination for Primary School Teachers: Each province and city should promote normal schools, simple normal schools, and simple normal school departments according to local needs to cultivate primary school teachers. They should also find ways to provide unqualified primary school teachers with opportunities for further study and obtain qualifications in accordance with the qualification examination regulations.

6. School Buildings and Equipment

Regarding school buildings and equipment, due to insufficient funding for compulsory education, we can only make do with what we have for the time being. However, funds must be raised to build formal school buildings and equipment for the future establishment of ordinary primary schools. The principles of school buildings and equipment are reported below:

(1) School Buildings: Short-term primary schools set up in each primary school district should make full use of local government offices, ancestral halls, and other buildings, or rent private houses. If there is nothing to rent, simple sheds may be temporarily built for use. Each school district should select a suitable location and prepare to build formal school buildings for ordinary primary schools within ten years. If they are unable to build, they may be assisted by the county and municipal governments.

(2) Equipment: The equipment for short-term primary schools should be handled with reference to the equipment for ordinary primary schools. Each school district should raise sufficient equipment funds within ten years to prepare for the conversion of short-term primary schools into ordinary primary schools.

7. Agencies for Implementing Compulsory Education

The implementation of compulsory education is organized by the Ministry of Education at the central level, by the education administrative agencies of provinces and cities at the provincial and municipal levels, and by the education departments and bureaus at the county and municipal levels. Each level of organizing agency should form a committee to assist in the implementation.

8. Principles of Rewards and Punishments

(1) The state of compulsory education implementation should be regarded as a special consideration when evaluating the performance of local administrative personnel.

(2) People who donate funds to support compulsory education may be rewarded in accordance with the regulations on rewarding donations for education.

(3) The Ministry of Education will separately formulate regulations on rewards and punishments for promoting compulsory education.

The measures for implementing compulsory education have been largely reported. The goal of compulsory education is to transform the environment, adapt to the environment, and increase the people's ability to live. Therefore, education must take into account the needs of society. China is a vast country with abundant resources, but transportation is inconvenient. Not only does each province have its own customs, habits, and languages, but each county and each place also has its own customs, habits, and languages. With such regional separation, people live in different environments, making it difficult to unite. Now, we must rely on the power of compulsory education to unify social customs and habits, so that everyone can have a common spirit from different living environments, and develop their production skills and increase their interest in life according to the needs of the time and place. Not only will there be no illiteracy in the country, but foolishness will be transformed into intelligence, poverty will be transformed into wealth, disease will be transformed into health, and sin will be transformed into light. With a whole and healthy citizenry, we can jointly shoulder the responsibility of saving the country and ensuring its survival. Why worry that the country cannot be strong and the nation cannot be revived? Therefore, I believe that compulsory education is the most fundamental and effective work for saving the country, ensuring its survival, and revitalizing the nation. I hope that all compatriots across the country will work together to assist the government. (End)

Fourth Meeting of the Literacy Education Committee 132

The Shanghai Municipal Literacy Education Committee held its fourth meeting yesterday at the Municipal Government. All members of the committee attended, chaired by Mayor Wu, the chairman. (1) Reporting items: (1) The committee's previous survey of illiterate people has now been statistically analyzed. Excluding a portion of children who have already been surveyed by the Municipal Education Bureau and are no longer included, the remaining number is 434,452, including 208,161 men and 226,291 women. (2) The committee's publicity and survey work this time has achieved good results, thanks to the assistance of many parties. A type of certificate has now been produced to reward them, and 68 certificates have been issued. (3) The committee's training for teachers of literacy schools was completed on schedule on June 23. In addition to dismissing two who performed poorly, the rest were assigned to various districts as teachers. The selection of temporary duty officers in each district was also completed by the committee on June 24. (4) The committee's first phase of 220 literacy schools, with more than 1,300 classes, opened on schedule on July 1. After repeated inspections by the Shanghai Municipal Government and the committee, the results are satisfactory. The number of students who actually attended last month is currently being statistically analyzed. (5) The committee's experimental work in the Jiangwan Experimental District has been completed and it has been converted into an ordinary district. Mr. Jiang Wenbao, the original director of the Experimental District, has resigned and Mr. Wu Chuijiu, a municipal committee member of the district, has been appointed to succeed him. The details of the district's experiment have been detailed in the special issue of this issue of the Education Magazine, and will not be repeated here. (6) Because of the special nature of labor literacy education, the committee has added a labor education section to the Secretariat, and appointed Mr. Wang Gang, director of the labor welfare section of the Third Bureau of the Social Affairs Bureau, to concurrently serve as the director of the section. Single measures have now been established to investigate illiteracy and urge factories to set up labor literacy classes on schedule. (7) The second volume of the adult literacy textbook and the second volume of the children's literacy textbook were both published last month and have been distributed for use. (8) Although more than 500 sub-teams of the literacy education service team have been established, the work situation is difficult to be optimistic. It is probably because it is during the summer vacation, and it is planned to step up supervision from September. (9) The committee's epidemic prevention campaign for students in literacy schools has begun, and the Health Bureau has sent personnel to administer vaccinations. (10) Various important regulations previously passed by the committee have been approved for record by the Shanghai Municipal Government and forwarded to the Ministry of Education. 2. Discussion items: 1. The draft interim measures for civic training are hereby submitted for review. Approved by resolution. 2. The rules for the study group of literacy schools are hereby submitted for review. Approved by resolution. 3. The 50 new life items in the classroom of literacy schools are hereby submitted for review. Approved by resolution. 4. The committee plans to subsidize each district office 1 yuan per school per month for the civic training held in each district, totaling 220 yuan per month and 3,420 yuan per year (calculated in November). It is proposed to submit this to the Municipal Government for approval. Approved by resolution. (5) The committee hereby formulates measures for the academic performance examination of students in literacy schools for review. Resolution: Appoint three members, Tao Baichuan, Hong Kui, and Tong Hangbai, to review. (6) Should the committee's literacy school teachers' winter uniforms be manufactured and distributed for review? It was resolved not to manufacture and distribute them again. (7) The salary of the committee's literacy school teachers was originally calculated based on the number of classes and the number of people taught. Those with more than 40 people will be given a salary of 6 yuan, 6 jiao, and 7 fen per class. However, how should the exact number of these 40 people be examined and verified, and how should the salary be paid for classes with less than 40 people in order to be fair? Please review the proposal. Resolution: It was decided to review and decide based on the roll call book of the literacy school. Those with less than 40 people will be paid generously in proportion. (8) Can the certificate of academic performance of students in private literacy schools under the guidance of the Municipal Party Department (that is, educational certificate) be issued by the committee for the Municipal Party Department to assess and forward, or should it still be forwarded by the district office? Please review the proposal. Resolution: It was decided to allow the Municipal Party Department to be responsible for the assessment and forwarding to the meeting for record. The meeting adjourned after the discussion.

Little Men (10) (1) 134

— Original by American Ms. Alcott, translated by Zheng Xiaocang (Zonghai)

Therefore, after dinner, when the children gathered in the classroom to do some more "fun things," Mrs. Pei also came slowly, with a violin in her hand. After saying a word to her husband, she went straight to Naide's side, who was sitting in a corner, watching with great interest.

"Now, my child, play a piece for us. Our orchestra just needs a violin, and I think you can play it well."

She thought he might hesitate, but he immediately took the old violin, holding it so carefully and lovingly that it was clear that music was his passion.

He only said, "Madam, I will do my best," and then touched the string with the bow, as if eager to hear the faint sound that had been silent for a long time again.

There was a lot of noise in the room, but Naide was oblivious to everything else. He just played for himself, extremely happy, and unaware of anything else. What he played was just a tune sung by a black man, which was often performed by street musicians, but this immediately attracted the children's attention, making them quiet down until they all stood listening intently, admiring in amazement. They gradually gathered around him, and Mr. Pei also came closer to observe carefully! Because Naide suddenly felt like a fish in water, he just played, losing all his shyness. Later, his eyes shone brightly, and his cheeks were as red as fire. His slender fingers danced back and forth on the strings, and he held the old violin tightly, borrowing it to speak directly to everyone's hearts in the language he loved most.

Wonderful Tennis Match Amid Continuous Applause, Xu Chengji Defeats Carlson, Xu's Technical Progress Show is Extremely Wonderful, Xu Lin Doubles Wins Carlson Shi Guiya, Xu Chengji vs. Qiu Feihai Today 135

Our country's Davis Cup player Xu Chengji defeated Carlson, last year's Shanghai singles champion and manager of our country's Davis Cup team, in continuous applause yesterday by two to one, with scores of 4-6, 6-3, and 6-4. The performance of both sides was extremely exciting and moving, and can be called the most wonderful tennis performance in Shanghai this season. Xu has made significant progress in technical hitting, and it is no wonder that the audience praised him and applauded thunderously. There was also a singles match in which Zhang Dingzhao defeated Luo Xiaojian two to zero. In the final doubles match, Xu Lin teamed up to defeat Carlson Shi Guiya without much effort. It rained yesterday morning until noon, so the audience was slightly reduced. Today, starting at 4 pm, Xu will fight Qiu Feihai on the same ground. Judging from yesterday's performance, victory should be easy. Yesterday's results are as follows:

Xu Chengji 4-6 6-3 6-4 Carlson

Zhang Dingzhao 6-2 6-2 Luo Xiaojian

Xu Chengji Lin Baohua 6-2 6-4 Carlson Shi Guiya

Significant Technical Progress

Xu Chengji not only performed wonderfully yesterday, but also his movements and postures were extremely moving. His serve was heavy and powerful, scoring many points. Mistakes are extremely rare. The serve is now very reliable. The cross-court exchanges are deep and extremely far, and the volleying at the net is wonderful everywhere. His backhand is powerful and is the most significant progress. Carlson is not a weak player, but Xu took the upper hand everywhere. He should have won the first set. He should also be able to win against Lin Qiu without a doubt. The current Xu is really not inferior to Japan's Hirai and others.

Carlson Wins the First Set First

Xu first opened the game, winning two consecutive games. The beauty of his sideline shots made Carlson unable to cope. In the next three games, Xu repeatedly tried to attack Carlson's backhand, but as a result, Carlson won instead, exceeding with a score of three to two. Xu's deep and distant cross-court exchanges and heavy serves also won back two games, and he was ahead with a score of four to three. The situation was extremely even, but because of the failure of Xu's service game in the ninth game, Carlson won the first set with a score of six to four.

Xu Chengji Overcomes Carlson

Xu Chengji was not flustered and was extraordinarily calm. Each won their service game to make the score two to two. Carlson broke Xu's serve and took the lead with a score of three to two. At this time, Xu suddenly saw a boost, and his diagonal cross-court shot was excellent, unmatched for a time. He completed it in one breath, winning four consecutive games and taking back the second set with a score of six to three. In the third set, Xu still had the upper hand, and his momentum was extremely good, four to two and then five to three, which had become a sure victory. He finally won the third set with a score of six to four.

Luo Xiaojian Cannot Defeat Zhang Dingzhao, the appearance of Luo Xiaojian Zhang Dingzhao eased the atmosphere a lot. Zhang Dingzhao's baseline shots and forehand heavy pressure made Luo Xiaojian unable to cope, and Luo's serves were heavy and overlapping, and double faults were uncountable. Only in the second game of the second set was there a fierce battle. As a result, Zhang won with two sets of six to two.

Xu Lin Doubles are a Perfect Match

The Xu Lin pairing in doubles can be called a perfect match. Both of them have fierce volleys and heavy serves. In addition, the opponent Shi Guiya is the weakest of the four. Carlson's efforts alone are of no avail. Lin Baohua even concentrated the ball point and hit Shi Guiya. The first set was six to two, and the second set was six to four, and neither had a fierce battle.

Commercial News

Finance: Major Players Continue to Aggressively Sell; Bullion Margin Loosens; Briefly Breaking the 900 Yuan Barrier; Finally Rebounding Six Yuan Seven Jiao 146

The gold market yesterday saw a loosening of the floor as major players from the previous days continued to sell off significant amounts, with a slightly stronger selling sentiment, making it easier for downstream participants. Major players continued to aggressively sell and also dumped foreign exchange, briefly falling below the 900 yuan mark. The Kuo Hwa Bank came in to buy US dollars, and rumors spread of a certain bank entering the market, sparking a reaction. However, the price ultimately fell due to predictions of a rise in printed silver. In the early morning, overseas silver markets were stable in both the UK and the US, while forward silver prices in Monterrey fell by 0.5 to 1 li. Exchange rates were normal, and the London gold spot price fell by half a penny. Market sentiment had already fallen overnight in the gray market due to Minister Kong's denial of inflation. When pre-market trading opened yesterday morning, it immediately retreated to around ten yuan, and soon fell further to 89 yuan. The shorts slightly covered, rising to 11-12 yuan. However, due to the continued sell-off by major long positions, the situation was difficult to improve. The price broke the ten yuan barrier immediately after opening. The Central Bank's official rate remained unchanged, and the supply surged, causing a downward trend. Banks took advantage of the cheap prices to buy in, resulting in some rebound, but failed to break through the ten yuan barrier. Later, although the HSBC official rate did not change, the domestic market strengthened due to the sale of foreign exchange by Cheng Lan Yong, and the price fell again. At this time, the price remained relatively stable due to the unremitting efforts of HSBC and others. However, it was ultimately unsustainable as Xingye took the opportunity to sell at a high price. After entering, the banks' appetite slowed down slightly, but the selling pressure increased, breaking through the 900 yuan barrier. Unexpectedly, the Shanghai Kuo Hwa Bank continued to buy in, and the price soon rebounded. Despite many struggles along the way, the demand from the mainland Kuo Hwa Bank was very strong, the foreign exchange market tightened, and market sentiment reacted, with buying sentiment returning. Rumors spread of a certain bank entering the market, causing the shorts to be squeezed and rush to cover, breaking through the ten yuan mark. The longs continued to supply, and the price of printed silver was predicted to rise by four annas, leading to a decline. However, there was support at the low price. At noon, the market turned sideways, and the overall trend for the first half of the day remained volatile. Major players entered and exited abruptly, causing market sentiment to be uncertain and creating large price swings, making it difficult to predict the future. The market conditions for the first half of the day are recorded below:

The opening price was 911 yuan and 2 jiao, falling 2 yuan and 8 jiao from the previous close, then 1 yuan and 8 jiao. The Central Bank's customs gold unit rate remained unchanged. The price fell to 05 yuan and 5 jiao. Yong Li, Wan Xing, Yuan Yi, Heng Yu, Fu Xing Yong took advantage of the low price to buy in. Wah 比 bought US dollars for September at 31.25, rising to 7 yuan and 8 jiao. Da Fa and Yong Wan Feng sold. The price fell to 5 yuan and 7 jiao. Fu Yu, Yong Li, Fu Xing Yong, Da De Cheng, Chun Yuan Yong entered again, rising to 9 yuan and 8 jiao. Fu Xing Yong, Fu Yu, Yuan Mao Yong supplied at a high price, retreating to 8 yuan. Fu Xing Yong and Hui Xiang entered again to 9 yuan and 4 jiao. Xingye came out with September US dollars 25. Chang Da, Fu An, Yi Yu, Heng Yu, Yi Feng, Yong Da Fa, Yong Yong Li, Da Da, Shen Feng sold. Spring and Autumn Children's Weekly

The Ten Demands of Children 158

— Bing Xin

The enthusiastic and great Children's Year has begun. The society and the nation will seek tangible happiness and infinite benefits for children across the country. Children are naturally excited, joyful, hopeful, and grateful. Taking advantage of this once-in-a-lifetime opportunity, the author, on behalf of children nationwide, presents ten demands for their lives:

First, there must be well-stocked children's libraries. -- Living in a complex society, we suffer from a knowledge famine and cannot develop; with a lack of learning, we are bound to be eliminated. Children's libraries are where we absorb knowledge and study. Dear society and nation, give us well-stocked children's libraries, quickly.

Second, there must be spacious children's playgrounds. -- Living in bustling cities, we are surrounded by dense populations and polluted air; our bodies are tired, and our spirits are stressed. Children's playgrounds are where we can rest our bodies and comfort our spirits. Dear society and nation, give us spacious children's playgrounds, quickly.

Third, there must be complete children's museums. -- School facilities may not be complete; knowledge on paper may not be correct. The objects displayed in children's museums can be observed, verified, and can provide practical knowledge at any time. Dear society and nation, give us complete children's museums, quickly.

Fourth, there must be suitable children's sports fields. -- To improve health, we must emphasize exercise; to develop physique, we must emphasize training. The equipment in children's sports fields can be used for us to learn, compete, and strengthen our muscles and bones at any time. Dear society and nation, give us suitable children's sports fields, quickly.

Fifth, there must be ordinary children's zoos. -- In the study of natural science, we must observe real objects to study various animals to create a deep impression. Therefore, there must be children's zoos, raising various birds, beasts, insects, and fish, for us to observe their forms, study their habits, and experiment with breeding methods. Dear society and nation, give us ordinary children's zoos, quickly.

Sixth, there must be scenic children's botanical gardens. -- In the study of natural science, we must also observe real objects to study various plants to avoid confusing concepts. Therefore, there must be children's botanical gardens, planting various beautiful flowers, exotic grasses, precious trees, and strange plants, for us to appreciate their forms, study their functions, and experiment with cultivation methods. Dear society and nation, give us scenic children's botanical gardens, quickly.

Seventh, there must be simple children's art museums. -- Art is the cultural crystallization of humanity. Art museums dedicated to our appreciation, displaying ordinary works, are enough to arouse a love of beauty, and artistic thoughts. Dear society and nation, give us simple children's art museums, quickly.

Eighth, there must be noble children's cinemas. -- Movies are ordinary leisure entertainment. Cinemas dedicated to our viewing, showing educational films, are enough to enhance the development of knowledge and interest in life. Dear society and nation, give us noble children's cinemas, quickly.

Ninth, there must be legitimate children's drama societies. -- Drama is an active art that can stir emotions and entertain the mind. Our drama societies, through our own activities, rehearse stories or songs and dances for children to watch. Dear society and nation, give us legitimate children's drama societies, quickly.

Tenth, there must be universal children's broadcasting groups. -- Broadcasting is an emerging art that can impart knowledge and report current events. Our broadcasting groups, allow us to work ourselves, broadcasting songs or speeches for children to listen to. Dear society and nation, give us universal children's broadcasting groups, quickly.

If these ten demands can be fully realized within this year, and if they are to be universal across the country and enjoyed by all, not limited to one area or class, then that will not betray the nation's intention in establishing Children's Year; that will truly be seeking tangible happiness and infinite benefits for us. Naturally, we must also strive to cultivate our character, improve our knowledge and abilities, and strengthen our physique, so that we can all become capable citizens who repay society and the nation.

The Story of Yu the Great Taming the Floods (History) 159

— Yang Chunlu

The Yangtze River and the Yellow River have simultaneously experienced major floods, with breaches and submergences in various places. Unfortunate news continues to come from newspapers. Thus, the issue of flood prevention and disaster relief has become the most urgent issue at present. Speaking of flood prevention and disaster relief, we are reminded of the story of Yu the Great taming the floods more than 4,000 years ago, which I will introduce to the children:

During the time of Emperor Yao, floods plagued various places. The floodwaters were extremely vast, even submerging hills and mountains, not to mention the plains. People lived in nests in trees or climbed high mountains, suffering from hunger and cold, and leading extremely difficult lives. Thus, Emperor Yao ordered Gun to tame the floods. He built dikes to defend against the floods, but the floodwaters were fierce, and the dikes could not withstand them, breaking as soon as they were built. So, after nine years of governance, the floods in China still could not be quelled. During the time of Emperor Shun, Gun was killed, and his son Yu was ordered to continue his father's duties and tame the floods again. Yu knew that his father's method of building dikes to resist the water was wrong, so he changed to a method of dredging and guiding the water, dredging the Yellow River, the Yangtze River, the Huai River, and the Han River, making them flow into the sea. He waded through water, climbed mountains, and travelled east and west, never taking a moment to rest. He passed his home three times in eight years without entering. Because he was so dedicated to taming the floods, the disaster of the floods was finally quelled.

Save the Children! (Current Affairs Talk) 160

— He Gongchao

The opening ceremony of Children's Year was held on August 1st in various places. How lively! How happy! However, in the newspapers of that day, we saw a tragic piece of news: A primary school teacher named Xu in the north, because he had lung disease, actually bought a child from a poor family and cooked him alive to eat.

Children, I am reporting this matter to you so that you know: (1) On the one hand, people are holding Children's Year, shouting "seek happiness for the children," while on the other hand, someone is taking a child to cook alive. This society is full of "contradictions." (2) As a primary school teacher, one should have a certain amount of knowledge; however, he actually thought that eating a child could cure lung disease. Medical knowledge is lacking to such an extent! If primary school teachers are like this, there is no need to mention the many people who have never read books. From this, we can know that most people in this society are still very "stupid." (3) In order to cure his own illness, he cooked someone else's child alive; people like this who only care about themselves and do not care about others are definitely not just one person, and incidents of this kind of heartlessness are definitely not just one. From this, we can know that many people in this society are "selfish" and "cruel." (4) Parents would never be willing to sell their own children to others unless it was absolutely necessary, let alone have them cooked alive. From this, we can know that the lives of many of our people are already "poor" to the extreme.

We are young and powerless children, born into a society full of contradictions, where the four fierce demons of "stupidity," "selfishness," "cruelty," and "poverty" are harming us at any time and in any place; but who is our savior?

We must unite, organize ourselves, and work together with the adults who are engaged in children's work to do the following: (1) help children in disaster areas, (2) help poor children, (3) establish labor nurseries, orphanages, and educational institutions, (4) participate in literacy campaigns, and instill common sense in the people.

Children, we live in this hellish society, we must awaken the adults to save the children, and we must awaken the children to save themselves!
